style=""><div><div class="standard-markdown grid-cols-1 grid [&amp;_&gt;_*]:min-w-0 gap-3 standard-markdown"><p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">A repo icon should be clean, scalable, and readable even when small, so SVG is the right primary format (GitHub renders it in READMEs and you can recolor it easily), with PNG exports for avatars/social previews. Let me design a compact vertical QC-pipeline icon: mixed raw reads (one flagged) → filter/funnel → clean aligned reads → a QC-pass check.</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">I'll define the geometry once and emit both the SVG and high-res PNGs from it so they stay identical.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-4"><div class="grid grid-rows-[auto_auto] min-w-0"><div class="row-start-1 col-start-1 min-w-0"><div data-find-omitted="" class="contents"><div class="min-w-0 pl-2 py-[var(--msg-pill-py,0.375rem)]"><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="group/status flex items-center gap-2 py-1 text-sm transition-colors cursor-pointer text-left text-text-500 hover:text-text-300 flex-1 min-w-0" aria-expanded="false"><div class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 min-w-0" style="opacity: 1;"><span class="truncate font-base">Validated icon visibility across multiple sizes and themes</span><span class="inline-flex -rotate-90 shrink-0 opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-200 group-hover/status:opacity-100 group-focus-visible/status:opacity-100"><div style="width: 12px; It reads as a QC pipeline top-to-bottom: mixed raw reads coming in (one amber read flagged as a contaminant/low-quality), passing through a filter funnel, and coming out as clean, aligned reads — with a green QC-pass check stamp.</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">A few notes for using it:</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">The SVG is the main asset — it's resolution-independent, tiny, and easy to recolor (the palette is at the top of the file as hex values, and the background is a <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">linearGradient</code> with id <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">bg</code>). GitHub renders SVG in READMEs, e.g. <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">&lt;img src="assets/icon.svg" width="120" alt="logo"&gt;</code>. The badge has its own dark rounded background, so it sits cleanly on both light and dark README themes. The 512 and 1024 PNGs are there for places that need raster (org/user avatars, Open Graph, etc.).</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">At very small sizes (≤32px) the funnel mesh and the flag mark get tiny; the two read clusters and the check still carry the meaning, but if you want a dedicated small/favicon variant I can strip it down to just funnel + check.</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">I can also generate a GitHub social-preview version (1280×640, icon + repo name), a transparent-background variant (no rounded card, for embedding on colored surfaces), or alternate color themes (e.g. all-teal, or a light-card version). Want any of those?</p></div></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-2 py-2"><div class="group/artifact-block relative flex text-left font-ui rounded-lg overflow-hidden border-0.5 transition duration-300 The icon now tells the whole story top to bottom: a microbial community (two flagellated rods + a coccus cluster, with the amber one flagged as a contaminant), feeding through the QC filter funnel, out to clean aligned reads with a green pass check, and the <strong>met</strong>qc wordmark anchoring the bottom (name split — "met" in off-white, "qc" in teal).</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">A couple of practical notes:</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">The "metqc" text is baked into the SVG as vector outlines (from Geist Mono), not live text, so it renders identically anywhere without needing the font installed. Colors are still all editable near the top of the file if you want to tweak them. Because the wordmark is small at tiny sizes, the graphic carries the meaning at favicon scale while the name reads fine at README/hero sizes (≥128px).</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">If useful, I can also produce a horizontal lockup (icon on the left, larger "metqc" beside it) for the README header, a text-free square version for favicons, or a 1280×640 GitHub social-preview banner. (The viewer was just showing placeholders this turn; the pixels confirm it's correct.)</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">I'll make the light/transparent version the primary <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">icon.*</code> and keep the dark card as <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">icon-dark.*</code> in case you ever want the framed app-icon look.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-4"><div class="grid grid-rows-[auto_auto] min-w-0"><div class="row-start-1 col-start-1 min-w-0"><div data-find-omitted="" class="contents"><div class="min-w-0 pl-2 py-[var(--msg-pill-py,0.375rem)]"><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><button class="group/status flex items-center gap-2 py-1 text-sm transition-colors cursor-pointer text-left text-text-500 hover:text-text-300 flex-1 min-w-0" aria-expanded="false"><div class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 min-w-0" style="opacity: 1;"><span class="truncate font-base">Ran a command, read a file</span><span class="inline-flex -rotate-90 shrink-0 opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-200 group-hover/status:opacity-100 group-focus-visible/status:opacity-100"><div style="width: 12px; height: 12px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true" style="flex-shrink: 0;"><path d="M14.128 7.165a.502.502 0 0 1 .744.67l-4.5 5-.078.07a.5.5 0 0 1-.666-.07l-4.5-5-.06-.082a.501.501 0 0 1 .729-.656l.075.068L10 11.752z"></path></svg></div></span></div></button></div><span class="sr-only" role="status" aria-live="polite">Ran a command, read a file</span><div class="grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-300 ease-out" style="grid-template-rows: 0fr;"><div class="overflow-hidden min-w-0"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="row-start-2 col-start-1 relative grid grid-rows-[auto_auto] isolate min-w-0"><div class="row-start-1 col-start-1 relative z-[2] min-w-0"><div style=""><div><div class="standard-markdown grid-cols-1 grid [&amp;_&gt;_*]:min-w-0 gap-3 standard-markdown"><p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">Retuned for a white background. <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">icon.svg</code> (plus the 512/1024 PNGs) is now the light version: transparent background, no dark card, with deeper colors so everything reads on white — dark teal-ink "met", teal "qc", deep-teal reads and funnel, and stronger emerald/blue/amber bacteria with a red contaminant flag. The PNGs are transparent, so they sit cleanly on your white README.</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal"><code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">icon-dark.svg</code> is the original framed dark-card version, kept as an alternative in case you want the app-icon look somewhere (e.g. a social-preview banner).</p>
<p class="font-claude-response-body break-words whitespace-normal">A couple of things worth noting: on a pure-white page the transparent version is ideal, but if your README ever renders in GitHub dark mode, the dark "met" text will nearly vanish — for that case GitHub supports theme-swapping with <code class="bg-text-200/5 border border-0.5 border-border-300 text-danger-000 whitespace-pre-wrap rounded-[0.4rem] px-1 py-px text-[0.9rem]">&lt;picture&gt;</code>:</p>

This forked repository has a few modifications from the original one, including some filtering steps, change of parameters and software, and modifying the Snakemake files linked to it.

The modifications include:
- `Cutadapt` replacement with `bbduk` (this change allows the user to not specify the exact sequence for the adapters, and it gets to remove polyGs and polyCs in the case of a NextSeq or NovaSeq instrument)
- 


What you need:
- A `logs` folder (found in this repository, so if you clone it you should be good)
- A `config.yaml` file with your specified parameters
- A `Snakefile` (best if you don't modify this one.
- A `cluster.json` file that can be used when submitting a Snakemake job in a Slurm-supported server

Versions we recommend for the pipeline to run just fine:
- Snakemake 7.32.4
- Bbduk 39.26
- FastQC v0.12.1
- MultiQC v1.0.dev0
- PRINSEQ-lite 0.20.4
- BBMap 39.26
- Bmtagger 1.1.0

Output:
Folders 
Files
